
In `session.py`, the session stores `todo_items`, but the `TodoList._items` never gets populated from it.

The fix needs to:
1. Create a shared `TodoList` instance
2. On session load, populate `TodoList._items` from `session.todo_items`
3. On session save, sync `TodoList._items` to `session.todo_items`

### [2026-07-03 23:15:54] AI

---

### [2026-07-03 23:15:57] AI

78/78 全部通过。修复完成。

**根因**：`create_todo_tool()` 每次都创建独立的内存 `TodoList`，和 `Session.todo_items` 没有任何同步——Session 文件虽然存了 todo 数据，但加载时没有灌给工具，保存时也没有从工具拉取。

**修复后数据流**：

```
启动 → Session.load() 恢复 todo_items
     → todo_list.restore_from(session.todo_items)  ← 灌入内存
     → 对话...
     → Orchestrator.save:
         session.todo_items = todo_list.get_items()  ← 拉取最新
         session.save()                              ← 写入文件
```

现在删掉旧 session 文件（旧格式不兼容），重新测试即可：

```bash
rm -rf .scratch/sessions/
python agent.py
```

添加待办 → 退出 → 重新打开 → 问"我有哪些todo"——不会再丢了。

### [2026-07-03 23:20:25] AI

[思考] The user wants to understand how the mock search works. Let me explain it clearly.

---

### [2026-07-03 23:20:30] AI

很简单，就两层：

### 1. Adapter 接口

```python
class SearchAdapter:          # 抽象接口
    def search(self, query: str) -> str: ...
```

任何实现 `search(query) -> str` 的类都能插入。

### 2. Mock 实现

```python
class MockSearchAdapter(SearchAdapter):
    def search(self, query: str) -> str:
        return (
            f"Search results for '{query}':\n"
            f"  1. Mock result A about {query}\n"
            f"  2. Mock result B about {query}\n"
            f"  3. Mock result C about {query}\n"
            f"\n(These are mock results...)"
        )
```

不做任何真实搜索——直接把 query 嵌入一段固定模板返回 3 条假结果。LLM 看到这些假结果后会基于"有结果"的前提生成回复。

### 替换为真实搜索

```python
class TavilyAdapter(SearchAdapter):
    def search(self, query: str) -> str:
        # 调真实 API...
        return real_results

# 用真实实现替换：
create_search_tool(adapter=TavilyAdapter())
```

或者修改 `_default_adapter`：

```python
from agent_from_zero.tools.search import _default_adapter, MockSearchAdapter
from your_impl import RealSearchAdapter

# 替换全局默认
import agent_from_zero.tools.search as s
s._default_adapter = RealSearchAdapter()
```

### 关键：全局单例

第 27 行的 `_default_adapter = MockSearchAdapter()` 是模块级单例——所有 search 工具调用共享同一个 adapter 实例。替换它就全局生效，不需要改其他代码。

---

### [2026-07-03 23:46:15] AI

[思考] The user wants automatic context compression when the context reaches max_size, while still supporting manual `/compact` at any time.

I already have:
1. Manual `/compact` command working
2. `build_context()` does truncation (not compression) when over max_size

Now I need to make the auto-compression use the LLM summarization (like the manual compact does) when context overflows during normal conversation flow.

The change is in `_run_loop()` and `_run_loop_stream()` — before building messages, check if context overflows, and if so, automatically call the compact logic before proceeding.

Let me look at the current flow:

In `_run_loop()`:
```python
messages = build_context(list(self._history), max_size=self._max_size)
```
This currently does truncation (not summary) when over max_size.

In `_run_loop_stream()`:
```python
messages = build_context(list(self._history), max_size=self._max_size)
```
Same.

The fix: before calling `build_context`, check if overflow. If yes, auto-compact before proceeding. The `compact()` method already handles the LLM summarization.

Let me update both `_run_loop()` and `_run_loop_stream()` to auto-compact when over max_size. I should also make sure we don't try to compact on the very first message (when there's almost no history).

Let me implement this.

### [2026-07-03 23:46:49] AI

[思考] 78/78 all pass. Let me summarize the change.

---

### [2026-07-03 23:46:51] AI

78/78 ALL GREEN。

改动很小——只在 `_run_loop()` 和 `_run_loop_stream()` 的 `build_context` 调用前加了 `self._auto_compact()`：

```python
# 之前：超限只做截断（丢旧消息）
messages = build_context(list(self._history), max_size=self._max_size)

# 现在：超限先调 LLM 摘要压缩，再 build
self._auto_compact()
messages = build_context(list(self._history), max_size=self._max_size)
```

`_auto_compact()` 逻辑：

- `context_size < max_size` → 什么都不做（零开销）
- 超限 → 调 LLM 摘要最早 50% 消息 → 替换原文 → stderr 输出一行 `[auto-compact: 95,421 → 42,180 chars]`
- LLM 调用失败 → 静默跳过，fallback 到原有截断

`/compact` 命令不受影响，任何时候都能手动触发。

---

### [2026-07-04 00:01:28] AI

[思考] Now I have the key information from the DeepSeek documentation. Let me summarize what I learned:

1. **Thinking is now available on `deepseek-chat` (V3/V4) models** — not just `deepseek-reasoner`. You enable it by passing `thinking: {"type": "enabled"}` in `extra_body`.

2. **Two key parameters**:
   - `thinking`: `{"type": "enabled"}` or `{"type": "disabled"}` — enables/disables thinking mode
   - `reasoning_effort`: `"high"` or `"max"` — controls thinking intensity

3. **Reasoning content in responses**:
   - Non-streaming: `response.choices[0].message.reasoning_content`
   - Streaming: `chunk.choices[0].delta.reasoning_content`

4. **Multi-turn rules**:
   - Without tool calls: DON'T include `reasoning_content` in the next turn's messages
   - With tool calls: MUST include `reasoning_content` in the assistant message, or 400 error

5. **Important**: Must use `extra_body={"thinking": {"type": "enabled"}}` with OpenAI SDK

Now let me plan the modifications:

### What needs to change:

1. **`deepseek_adapter.py`**:
   - Add `thinking: {"type": "enabled"}` in `extra_body` for both `chat()` and `chat_stream()`
   - Add `reasoning_effort` support (optional, default to `high`)
   - In `chat()`: capture `reasoning_content` from the message (already partially done)
   - In `chat_stream()`: capture `reasoning_content` from delta chunks (already partially done)
   
2. **`orchestrator.py`**:
   - When building assistant messages WITHOUT tool_calls: strip `reasoning_content` (per docs: "无工具调用时不需要回传")
   - When building assistant messages WITH tool_calls: MUST include `reasoning_content` (already needs it but we weren't capturing it before)
   - Display thinking in REPL (already works for streaming)

3. **`orchestrator.py` — critical fix**:
   - In `_run_loop()` and `_run_loop_stream()`, when adding assistant messages to history:
     - If NO tool_calls: store content only, no reasoning
     - If HAS tool_calls: store content + reasoning
   - This is the key rule from the docs

4. **`system-prompt.md`** or CLI: Add `--thinking` flag to enable/disable thinking mode

5. **Default behavior**: Enable thinking by default (since it's on by default in the API)

Let me now present the modification plan to the user.

---

### [2026-07-04 00:01:33] AI

好，我已经通过搜索结果获取了 DeepSeek Thinking Mode 文档的关键内容。以下是我的修改计划。

---

## DeepSeek Thinking Mode — 关键发现

1. **`deepseek-chat` 就支持 thinking** —— 不限于 `deepseek-reasoner`。只需在请求中传 `extra_body={"thinking": {"type": "enabled"}}`
2. **两个新参数**：`thinking`（开关，默认开）+ `reasoning_effort`（`high` / `max`）
3. **多轮对话有严格规则**：
   - 无 tool_calls 时：**不要**在历史消息中回传 `reasoning_content`（API 会忽略）
   - 有 tool_calls 时：**必须**在 assistant 消息中保留 `reasoning_content`，否则 400 错误

---

## 修改计划

### 1. [deepseek_adapter.py](src/agent_from_zero/llm/deepseek_adapter.py)

| 改动 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| `__init__` 加 `reasoning_effort` 参数 | 默认 `high`，可选 `max` |
| `chat()` 加 `extra_body={"thinking": {"type": "enabled"}}` | 启用思考模式 |
| `chat()` 捕获 `reasoning_content` | 返回 `LLMResponse(thinking=...)` ✅ 已完成 |
| `chat_stream()` 加 `extra_body` + 捕获 `reasoning_content` | 流式也启用 |

### 2. [orchestrator.py](src/agent_from_zero/orchestrator.py)

| 改动 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| 纯文本 assistant 消息：**不带** `reasoning_content` | 遵守 API 规则，避免被忽略时的无效传输 |
| tool_calls assistant 消息：**带** `reasoning_content` | 遵守 API 规则，避免 400 错误 |
| `_auto_compact()` 写 `extra_body` 时也启用 thinking | 压缩时的摘要质量更高 |
| REPL 已支持显示 thinking ✅ | 无需改动 |

### 3. [agent.py](agent.py) + [cli.py](src/agent_from_zero/cli.py)

| 改动 | 说明 |
|------|------|
| 加 `--thinking` CLI 参数 | 默认 `on`，可选 `off` |
| 加 `--reasoning-effort` CLI 参数 | 默认 `high`，可选 `max` |

### 4. 不加的

- 不改默认模型（保持 `deepseek-chat`，thinking 模式对 chat 模型也生效）
- 不改变 REPL 显示逻辑（已经正确处理 `("thinking", ...)` 事件）

---

接受这个计划？

### 修改总结

| 文件 | 改动 |
|------|------|
| [deepseek_adapter.py](src/agent_from_zero/llm/deepseek_adapter.py) | `_build_kwargs()` 统一构建请求参数，含 `extra_body={"thinking": {"type": "enabled"}}` + `reasoning_effort` |
| [orchestrator.py](src/agent_from_zero/orchestrator.py) | `_execute_tools()` 中 assistant 有 tool_calls 时保留 `reasoning_content`；`_run_loop_stream()` 累积 `thinking_accumulated` |
| [cli.py](src/agent_from_zero/cli.py) | 新增 `--thinking`（默认 on，`--thinking off` 关闭）和 `--reasoning-effort`（`high` / `max`） |
| [agent.py](agent.py) | 接线 `thinking` 和 `reasoning_effort` 到 adapter |

### 现在的行为

- **默认启动就输出思考过程**（`deepseek-chat` + `thinking: enabled`）
- 思考过程在 stderr 灰色显示，正文流式输出在 stdout
- 符合 DeepSeek 多轮规则：纯文本不带 `reasoning_content`，有 tool_calls 时保留

```bash
# 默认：思考模式开启
python agent.py

# 关闭思考模式（更快、更省 token）
python agent.py --thinking off

# 最大思考强度
python agent.py --reasoning-effort max
```
